		<script>
    $(document).ready(function(){

        $("#add_form").validate({

            errorElement: 'span', //default input error message container
            errorClass: 'error', // default input error message class
            focusInvalid: false, // do not focus the last invalid input
            ignore: ".ignore",  // validate all fields including form hidden input

            highlight: function (element) { // hightlight error inputs
               
                if ($(element).attr("type") == "checkbox") {
                    var parent = $(element).closest('.field').parent();
                    parent.addClass('has-error'); // set error class to the control group
                } else if ($(element).attr("type") == "radio") {
                    var parent = $(element).closest('.field').parent().parent().parent();
                    parent.addClass('has-error'); // set error class to the control group
                } else {
                    $(element).closest('.field').addClass('has-error'); // set error class to the control group  
                } 
            },
           
            unhighlight: function (element) { // revert the change done by hightlight
                
                if ($(element).attr("type") == "checkbox") {
                    var parent = $(element).closest('.field').parent();
                    parent.removeClass('has-error'); // set error class to the control group
                } else if ($(element).attr("type") == "radio") {
                    var parent = $(element).closest('.field').parent().parent().parent();
                    parent.removeClass('has-error'); // set error class to the control group
                } else {
                    $(element).closest('.field').removeClass('has-error'); // set error class to the control group  
                }             
            },
            
            errorPlacement: function(error, element) {  

                element.parent().find('.error').remove();
                
                if (element.attr("type") == "checkbox") {
                    error.insertAfter(element.closest('.field').next());
                } else if (element.attr("type") == "radio") {
                    error.insertAfter(element.closest('label').next());
                } else {
                    if(element.parent('.input-group').length) {
                        error.insertAfter(element.parent());
                    } else {
                        error.insertAfter(element);
                    }
                }
            },

            success: function (label) {
                
                label.closest('.field, .checkbox').removeClass('has-error'); // set success class to the control group
            },

            submitHandler: function (form) {

                if(typeof Promotions != "undefined") {
                    if(Promotions.cancelSubmit()) {
                        return false;
                    }
                }

                var img = document.getElementById('images');
                if(img) {
                    img.setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');
                }

                // tag manager
                window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
                window.dataLayer.push({
                    'event' : 'newAdSuccess',
                    'formId' : 'AdaugaAnunt'
                });

                form.submit();

                var submitButton = document.getElementById('insert_new');
                if (submitButton) {
                    submitButton.setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');
                    setTimeout(function(){
                        submitButton.setAttribute('disabled', '');
                    }, 7000);
                }
            },

            invalidHandler: function(form, validator) {

                if(!validator.numberOfInvalids()) {
                    return;
                }

                if(validator.errorList && validator.errorList[0]){
                    var toGo = validator.errorList[0].element;
                    if(toGo.name == 'gmap') {
                        toGo = document.getElementById('gmap');
                    } else if (toGo.name == 'currency'){
                        toGo = document.getElementById('lei_holder');
                    }
                }
                
                if(toGo){
                    if (_.hasClass(document.body, 'sticky_menu')) { 
                        var topValue = $(toGo).offset().top - 82;
                    } else {
                        if(typeof isMobile !== 'undefined') {
                            var topValue = $(toGo).offset().top - 76;
                        } else {
                            var topValue = $(toGo).offset().top - 22;
                        }
                        
                    }           

                    $('html, body').animate({
                        scrollTop: topValue
                    }, 500);

                    setTimeout(function () {
                        if (typeof validator.errorList[0] !== 'undefined') {
                            $(validator.errorList[0].element).focus();
                        }
                    }, 500);
                }
            },
